				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Herr, gehe nicht ins Gericht mit deinem Knecht, BWV 105 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1723 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Herr, gehe nicht ins Gericht
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Lord, do not pass judgment on Your servant
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 105&#160;; BC A 114
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 284
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>G minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements:
<ol><li>Chorus: Herr, gehe nicht ins Gericht mit deinem Knecht  (G&#160;minor)
</li><li>Recitative (alto): Mein Gott, verwirf ich nicht (C&#160;minor-B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (soprano): Wie zittern und wanken der Sünder Gedanken (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitative (bass): Wohl aber dem, der seinen Bürgen weiß (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major-E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (tenor): Kann ich nur Jesum mir zum Freunde machen (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li>Chorale: Nun, ich weiß, du wirst mir stillen, mein Gewissen, das mich plagt (G&#160;minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1723 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1723-07-25 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1830 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
<dl><dd>Psalm CXLIII: 2 (No.1)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Anonymous" title="Category:Anonymous">Anonymous</a> (Nos.2-5)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Rist,_Johann" title="Category:Rist, Johann">Johann Rist</a> (1607-1667) (No.6)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>9th Sunday after Trinity
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>25 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>

<td><i>Voices:</i> soprano, alto, tenor, bass; mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> 2 oboes, horn, strings, continuo
